                                    looks like it is being called chapter 38, not 41. </note>

                                <note resp="Vandana Lele">
                                    <list>
                                        <item>1) I have doubt about the chapter number as
                                            the colophon of the manuscript mentions:
                                            "uttaratantre'ṣṭapañcāśattamaḥ kāyacikitsāyāṃ
                                            yonivyāpaccikitsā trayoviṅśatitamo'dhyāyaḥ
                                            samāptaḥ ||" As I have understood it, the
                                            above heading is given to the subject of this
                                            mail . I have also marked the same in the
                                            transcription file. Please comment.</item>
                                        <item>2) The folios which I have transcribed i.e
                                            480r:3, 480v, 481r, 481v are not
                                            paginated.</item>
                                        <item>3) Missing verses: 6.38.2, 3, 4, 5ab, 5cd,
                                            5, 6, 7, 6.38.30ab, 32cd, 32ef Probably,
                                            6.38.4.1 is left out to mark in the vulgate
                                            copy, like other verses 6.38.3.1, 6.38.2 etc.
                                            which are in manuscript. I am not sure about
                                            this observation. In vulgate, verse number
                                            6.38.8.1 is shown as missing but in manuscript
                                            I could not find different text relating to
                                            that for addition. (Here, also I may be
                                            wrong.)</item>
                                        <item>4) Additions: 6.38.3.1, 3.2, 4.1, 5.1, 6.1,
                                            7.1</item>
                                        <item>5) SS. 6.38.8cd, 17 cd , 23cd, 26cd, 27cd -
                                            the second half has different text.</item>
                                        <item>6) SS.6.38.28 ab - the first half has
                                            different text.</item>
                                    </list>
                                </note>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.44.1"><pb n="3422V"/>
                        <lb n="1"/>athātaḥ pāṇḍurpgapratiṣedhaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>

                        ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.44.3">pāṇdvā<lb n="2"/>mayoṣṭārddhavidhaḥ pradiṣṭaḥ
                        pṛthaksamastair yugapac ca doṣaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sarvve<cb/>ṣu caivaṣvihapāṇḍabhāvo yato 'dhikotaḥ khalu
                        pāṇḍurogaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.44.4">tvaksphoṭaṣṭhīvanagātrasāda mṛdbhakṣaṇa<lb n="3"
                        />prekṣaṇakūṭaśothāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         viṇmūtrapītatvamathāvipāko bhaviṣya<cb/>tastasya puras sarāṇi
                        ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.44.5">sa kāmalāpānnakipāṇḍurogaḥ kumbhāhvayo
                        lākarakolasākhyaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         vibhā<lb n="4"/>ṣyate lakṣaṇamasya kṛtsnaṃ nivodhya
                        vakṣyāmnupūrvvaśaste || <cb/>
                    </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.44.6">kṛṣṇekṣaṇaṃ kṛṣṇasirāvanaddhan tad
                        varṇaviṇmūtranakhānanañ ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         vātena pāṇḍum manujaṃ vyavasye dyuktan ta<lb n="5"/>thānyais tad
                        upadravaiś ca ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.44.7">pītekṣaṇaṃ pītasirāvanaddhaṃ tad
                        varṇṇa<cb/>viṇmūtranakhānanñ ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         pittena pāṇḍum manujam vyavasye dyuktaṃn tathānyais tad
                        ūpadravaiś ca ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.44.8">śukle kṣaṇaṃ śu<lb n="6"/>klasirāvanaddhan tad
                        varṇṇaviṇmūtranakhānanañ ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         kaphena pāṇḍum manujaṃ vyavasye dhyuktan tathānyais tad
                        upadravaiś ca ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.44.9">abhaktarūgnair avagātra sādāḥ sarvveṣu tandrī ca
                        valaksayañ ca |<pb n="3422R"/>
                        <lb n="1"/>
                        <caesura/>
                         sarvvātmake sarvvamidaṃ vyavasyelliṃgāni vakṣyāmyatha kāmalāyāḥ
                        ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.44.10">sahasānnamamla madyādapathyāni ca tasya pittaṃ
                        |
                        <caesura/>

                        tandrivalakṣayau ca ||</l>

                        mahān tatra ca parvvabhedaḥ |
                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.44.12">tam vāta<lb n="3"/>pittāddharipītanīlaṃ
                        halīmaketi pravadanti kecit ||
                        <caesura/>
                         upa<cb/>dravāsteṣvarūciḥ pipāsā charddirjvarāḥ śīrṣaujāgni sādaḥ

                        <lb n="6"/>uttaratantre trayaḥpañcāśattamaḥ kāyacikitsāyām
                        udāvarttacikitsāṣṭādaśamo 'dhyāyaḥ || ❈ ||</p>
